- [#816] ADR-034 Phase 1.2 — PTY backend for the embedded coding agent. New `src/scieasy/ai/agent/terminal.py` exposes a cross-platform `PtyProcess` wrapper (pywinpty on Windows, `pty.openpty()` + `subprocess.Popen` on POSIX) with `spawn_claude` and `spawn_codex` factories; pass Ctrl+C bytes through verbatim, normalise winpty's `str` reads to bytes, kill the process tree via `taskkill /T /F` (Win) or `os.killpg` (POSIX). New `src/scieasy/ai/agent/system_prompt.py` restores the `compose_system_prompt` helper (rolled back in PR #808) — reads `skills/scieasy/SKILL.md` and re-renders the `<!-- tool_catalog -->` block from the live `TOOL_REGISTRY`. New `src/scieasy/api/routes/ai_pty.py` hosts the locked-contract WebSocket route `ws://host/api/ai/pty/{tab_id}` (JSON frames `stdin`/`resize` → server, `stdout`/`exit`/`error` → client) with a hard cap of 16 concurrent terminals and pop-first teardown so the registry is consistent even when Starlette cancels the route coroutine mid-cleanup. New `GET /api/ai/status` in `src/scieasy/api/routes/ai.py` returns the locked `{providers: [{name, available, version, logged_in}, ...]}` shape, bounded by 2 s subprocess timeouts. `pywinpty>=2.0` added as a `sys_platform == 'win32'` conditional dep. 20 new tests (`tests/ai/test_terminal.py`, `tests/ai/test_system_prompt.py`, `tests/api/test_ai_pty.py`, `tests/api/test_provider_discovery.py`) cover PTY lifecycle / resize / kill_tree, system-prompt composition, the WS protocol end-to-end (lifecycle, resize, invalid provider, 16-cap, missing param), and the discovery endpoint (shape, missing binaries, timeout, claude credentials.json + macOS Keychain, codex auth.json). Frontend xterm.js terminal UI is built in parallel under a separate issue. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: feat/issue-816/phase-1-2-pty-backend, session: 20260513-204315-adr-034-phase-1-2-pty-backend)

### Fixed

- [#962 #909] Eliminate TOCTOU race between AI Block MCP-signal writer and `CompletionWatcher` reader. `tests/blocks/ai/conftest.py::StubAgent._emit` was writing `signals/finish_ai_block.json` (and the sibling `mark_done.json` + deliberate-error file) via `Path.write_text`, which opens the target with mode `"w"` and **truncates to 0 bytes before** writing data. The watcher polling on the main thread had a non-zero chance of reading the 0-byte file inside that window and re-raising `json.JSONDecodeError("Expecting value: line 1 column 1 (char 0)")` as `ValueError("AIBlock completion: malformed MCP signal …")`. This surfaced as ~1-in-30 flakes on Python 3.11 (occasionally 3.13) across all AIBlock skeleton tests — repeatedly hit during the ADR-038 / ADR-039 cascade (PR #926, #931, #940, #944) and cleared only by `gh run rerun --failed`. Issue #909 tracked the first-noticed symptom. Fix replaces the three non-atomic writes in `_emit` with a shared `_atomic_write_signal` helper using `tempfile.mkstemp` + `os.replace` (mirrors the existing production `scieasy.ai.agent.mcp.tools_workflow._atomic_write_text` pattern). Production `mcp__scieasy__finish_ai_block` already used the atomic helper, so no production write site changed — confirmed via `grep finish_ai_block src/`. The non-atomic `mark_done.json` write in `api/ws.py:118` was left as-is because `completion.py:218` swallows JSON errors on that path via `contextlib.suppress`. New `tests/blocks/ai/test_completion_race.py` ships two deterministic regression tests coordinated with `threading.Event`: `test_non_atomic_writer_loses_race` drives a buggy writer and asserts the watcher raises `ValueError` (documents the failure mode); `test_atomic_writer_wins_race` drives the atomic writer and asserts the watcher returns a `MCP_FINISH_TOOL` event cleanly (regression lock). Verified `pytest tests/blocks/ai/ tests/ai/` 57+ pass with no flakes. Checklist row "AI Block MCP-signal write/read race" in `docs/planning/adr-038-039-checklist.md` flipped to RESOLVED. Reader-side retry (option C in the checklist) intentionally NOT taken — it would weaken the watcher contract and mask future real writer-crash bugs. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: fix/issue-962/ai-block-atomic-signal-write, session: 20260515-160655-fix-962-atomic-write-for-aiblock-mcp-sig)
- [#898 #899] Data Preview panel — source filename in pill labels + single-slider 3-D viewer. **#898** (frontend-only): `extractRefEntries` walks `blockOutputs[block_id]` and resolves each `data_ref` to a friendly display name from `metadata.framework.source` (LoadImage) → `metadata.meta.source_file` (typed Image.Meta) → `metadata.meta.file_path` (Artifact) → truncated-ref fallback. Pill at `DataPreview.tsx:552` renders the filename (e.g. `1000nm_2800-3200-40.tif`) instead of `data-873de`. **#899**: `runtime.py::preview_data` image branch rewritten to (a) read `axes` from the wire format (set by `_serialise_extra_metadata` in `core/types/array.py`), (b) pick the (y, x) plane via axis labels or numpy convention (last two dims), (c) select the first non-(y, x) dim as the slider axis, (d) accept `?slice=N` query param (clamped to `[0, size-1]`, never 400), (e) emit `shape` as the FULL original ndim plus `axes`, `slice_axis_name`, `slice_axis_size`, `slice_index`. Frontend renders a horizontal `<input type="range">` slider in `ImageViewer` when `slice_axis_size > 1`, labeled e.g. `lambda (40)` with position `[N+1]/total`; 200 ms debounce on drag; local `sliceCacheRef: Map<refSliceKey, DataPreviewResponse>` for instant re-drag to cached positions. Zoom / pan / LUT / min-max display state persists across slice transitions because `ImageViewer` is never unmounted — the preview memo falls back to ANY cached slice for the same ref while a new slice is in flight, and the slider position is driven from parent `currentSliceByRef` state (not from `preview.slice_index`, which would snap back to a stale value). New spec at `docs/specs/data-preview-3d-viewer.md` documents the contract, the (y, x) detection precedence, and the v2 deferred items (RGB composite, multi-slider for ndim>3, lambda-click-spectrum, zarr partial reads). 5 new pytest cases in `tests/api/test_data.py` (ndim=2, (y,x,c), (z,y,x), no-axes fallback, `?slice=` clamping); 3 new vitest cases in `frontend/src/components/DataPreview.test.tsx` (filename pill resolution, slider rendered when `slice_axis_size > 1`, no slider for ndim=2). Live-verified via Chrome MCP in `microplastic-calibration`: `srs_calibrate` Done (`(40, 320, 320)` `axes=["lambda","y","x"]`) shows pills `1000nm_2800-3200-40.tif` etc., badge `40 × 320 × 320 | 100%`, slider `lambda (40) 13/40` after drag to position 12, image `src` changes between positions, zoom 156% and viridis LUT survive the drag; `max_project` Done (`(320, 320)`) shows no slider and badge `320 × 320 | 100%`. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: feat/issue-899/preview-panel-3d-viewer, session: 20260515-022426-preview-panel-source-filename-in-pills-3)
- [#879] Scaffold `workflows/main.yaml` on `POST /api/projects/` so the default "main" canvas tab has a real on-disk file from the moment a project is created. Previously the GUI showed an empty `main` tab purely in memory until the user pressed Ctrl+S — breaking View source (#878), file-watcher rehydration, and agent/MCP "what's in this project" introspection. `src/scieasy/api/runtime.py::create_project` now calls `save_yaml(WorkflowDefinition(id="main"), …/workflows/main.yaml)` after creating the directory tree, wrapped in best-effort try/except so a scaffold-write failure does not block project creation. Regression test in `tests/api/test_projects.py` asserts `workflows/main.yaml` exists and matches the canonical serializer shape. Live-verified via API + filesystem: `POST /api/projects/` returns `workflow_count: 1, workflows: ["main"]` and `main.yaml` is on disk. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/2026-05-15-session, session: n/a-hotfix-no-gate)
- [#878] View source on a fresh-but-unsaved workflow no longer pops a native `alert("<id> 不存在")`. The `onViewSource` handler in `frontend/src/App.tsx` now `await`s `saveWorkflow()` before calling `openFileTab(workflows/<id>.yaml, {readOnly: true})` so the YAML always exists on disk at open time. Native `alert()` was automation-hostile (blocks Chrome MCP) and a poor UX. Together with #879, the natural "new project → View source" path now works end-to-end. Live-verified via Chrome MCP: hooked `window.alert`, clicked View source on a brand-new project; `alerts: []` (no native alert fired) and the "main.yaml (source)" tab opened with content rendered. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/2026-05-15-session, session: n/a-hotfix-no-gate)
- [#871] CodeEditor lint responses now carry a request-version guard so out-of-order arrivals cannot repaint stale markers. `frontend/src/components/CodeEditor.tsx::runLint` bumps a monotonic `lintRequestIdRef` per scheduled lint, tags each in-flight request, and discards responses (both pre- and post-JSON-parse) whose tag is below the latest. Live-verified via Chrome MCP: mocked `/api/lint/python` so request #1 (3s delay, code `STALE1`) returns AFTER request #2 (0.5s delay, code `LATEST2`); Monaco model markers show only `LATEST2`. Without the guard, request #1's response would have overwritten #2. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/2026-05-15-session, session: n/a-hotfix-no-gate)
- [#870] File-tab autosave debounce timers now live in a `useRef<Map>` outside the effect closure, so editing one tab no longer cancels every other dirty tab's pending save. The previous `useEffect` had `[tabs]` as a dep and tore down all timers on every keystroke; continuously typing in tab A meant tab B's 800ms debounce never reached zero. The rewrite in `frontend/src/App.tsx` prunes only timers for tabs that are no longer dirty/present and resets a per-tab timer only when its OWN content changes. A separate unmount-only effect clears the map defensively. Live-verified via Chrome MCP: opened `blocks/foo.py` + `blocks/bar.py`; made bar dirty once; rapid-typed in foo (100ms cadence for 1.5s); `PUT /file?path=blocks/bar.py` fired at T+~0.8s (during foo-typing) and `PUT /file?path=blocks/foo.py` fired at T+~2.3s (after typing stopped). Before fix, bar.py would never have been saved during foo-typing. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/2026-05-15-session, session: n/a-hotfix-no-gate)
- [#869] `openFileTab` now refetches when an existing tab is stuck in `loading: true` (e.g. after `localStorage` rehydrate strips `content` and sets `loading: true` per ADR-036 §3.11). The previous early dedup-return left the rehydrated placeholder permanently empty. New `needsRefetch = existing && kind === "file" && loading` falls through to focus the existing slot, fire the GET, and replace the placeholder with populated content on success. Repopulation reads the current tab from store at `.then()` time so the path is identical for fresh-create and refetch. Live-verified via Chrome MCP: patched `fetch` to delay `/file` 4s, clicked View source, switched to canvas tab, clicked View source again while source tab was still loading — second click fired a second `GET /api/projects/{id}/file?path=workflows%2Fmain.yaml` (refetch path) instead of returning early. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/2026-05-15-session, session: n/a-hotfix-no-gate)
- [#883 #884] ADR-035 hotfix-2 — variadic AI Block port config + MCP env propagation. (1) `src/scieasy/engine/runners/worker.py:266` now instantiates the block as `block_cls(config=config)` instead of `block_cls()`; the previous form left `self.config = BlockConfig()` empty so variadic-port blocks (ADR-029 D1) read the static class-level `result` port instead of the user-configured `metadata` port from `self.config["output_ports"]`, and the CompletionWatcher / output validator monitored the wrong file (#883). (2) Engine-initiated PTY spawn now threads `extra_env` from `open_engine_initiated_tab` → `_spawn` → `spawn_claude` / `spawn_codex` → `PtyProcess.__init__`, injecting `SCIEASY_AI_BLOCK_RUN_DIR=str(run_dir_path)` into the child env; the `finish_ai_block` MCP tool's `_resolve_ai_block_run_dir()` already checked this env var but it had no producer, so every call returned `not_in_ai_block_context` and ADR-035 §3.5 path (a) was dead-on-arrival (#884). Validated live in ADR-035 e2e (4-image LoadImage → AIBlock → Save): manifest declares the user-config `metadata` port, FileWatcher (path b) detects `outputs/metadata.csv`, SaveData writes `metadata_saved.csv` with the expected rows. Path a (MCP `finish_ai_block`) plumbing is correct but runtime-unverified this round — Anthropic API was 529 Overloaded throughout the test window so claude could not invoke any tools. (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: hotfix/adr-035-port-config-and-mcp-tool, session: 20260514-205138-hotfix-2-ai-block-port-config-mcp-env-pr)
- [#880] ADR-035 hotfix — three live-debug fixes for the AI Block PTY path. (1) **CLI exports `SCIEASY_ENGINE_API_URL`** before uvicorn forks workers (`scieasy/cli/main.py` `gui` + `serve`) — companion to the `SCIEASY_ENGINE_IPC_TOKEN` export from #873 audit P1-B. Before this, every AIBlock crashed at PTY spawn with `RuntimeError: AIBlock: PTY spawn failed: request_pty_tab: SCIEASY_ENGINE_API_URL is not set` because workers had no way to call back to the engine for tab allocation. (2) **AIBlock inline node UI reordered**: `user_prompt` (textarea) + `provider` + `permission_mode` now have `ui_priority` 1/2/3 so they render on the canvas card; `input_ports` / `output_ports` lose their `ui_priority` and fall back to the side-panel port editor (where the editor has room). Previously the canvas card showed the two `[object Object]` port-editor strings + provider — useless for actually authoring the agent's task. (3) **`_scieasy_command_for_env` switches from `shutil.which("scieasy")` to `(sys.executable, ["-m", "scieasy"])`** so `<project>/.scieasy/mcp.json` always pins the same scieasy install as the engine — previously a stale `.venv-agent-test\Scripts\scieasy.EXE` on PATH would pin the wrong scieasy in every project's mcp.json and claude's MCP bridge silently failed (visible to user as "MCP servers failed" inside the AI Block PTY, killing path (a) of ADR-035 §3.5). Live e2e in Chrome confirmed: PTY spawn no longer crashes, canvas card shows the right fields, claude TUI no longer reports MCP server failures. CLAUDE.md §11.5 also gains an "on entering hotfix mode" rule (must re-read the relevant ADR + arch docs before any code edit, to ground against hallucination — gate workflow's change-plan checkpoint is suspended in hotfix mode so this is the only ground-truth pass). Out of scope and tracked separately: #881 prompt auto-submit (claude TUI consumes `\r`s for first-run welcome banners, no clean fix today), #882 conditional-AND completion semantics (ADR-035 §3.5 amend), #883 `get_effective_output_ports` doesn't see user-config ports (Mark done validator looks at static-default port), #884 scieasy MCP `finish_ai_block` tool not surfaced to claude despite bridge starting. (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: hotfix/adr-035-pty-spawn-and-block-ui, session: 20260514-182017-hotfix-adr-035-pty-spawn-env-block-inlin)
- [#852] ADR-035 Phase 2.6 — fix audit P1 + P2 (5 P1 + 1 P2). Addresses all findings from `docs/audit/2026-05-14-1253-adr-035-implementation.md`: (P1-A) `AIBlock._build_spawn_argv` re-raises bootstrap failures so the block transitions to ERROR with "AIBlock bootstrap failed: …" instead of silently degrading argv; (P1-B) `_ensure_ipc_token()` is now invoked from the FastAPI lifespan in `api/app.py` so `SCIEASY_ENGINE_IPC_TOKEN` is exported BEFORE any AI Block worker subprocess inherits the env — prior every internal IPC call returned 401 and the entire AI Block path was dead-on-arrival; (P1-C) `pty_endpoint` now JOINs an engine-pre-spawned PTY (detected via the `_engine_block_run_id` sentinel set by `open_engine_initiated_tab`) instead of calling `_spawn` a second time and orphaning the original agent process; on first WS connect it replays the recorded `_engine_initial_stdin` exactly once via a stamped sentinel attribute; (P1-D) `useWebSocket.ts::block_pty_closed` reads the top-level `event` field (the actual wire shape) and maps `completed → done` / `cancelled_by_user_close → cancelled` / `error → error` — successful runs no longer render as red ✗; (P1-E) `api/ws.py` now handles `block_user_marked_done` and `block_user_cancel` inbound frames by writing `signals/mark_done.json` under the right run dir; new `_engine_run_to_run_dir` registry + `PtyTabSpec.run_dir_path` field let the WS layer resolve `block_run_id → run_dir` without leaking AI Block internals into `api/ws.py`; (P2-A) `useWebSocket.ts::block_pty_opened` reads `permission_mode` from the top level (matching the engine's emit shape) so bypass-mode tabs register as `dangerous` instead of silently downgrading to `safe`. Tests: 6 new pytest cases in `tests/api/test_ai_pty_audit_fixes.py` (P1-A through P1-E + unknown-rid robustness) + 4 new vitest cases in `frontend/src/hooks/useWebSocket.test.ts` (P1-D ×3 mappings + P2-A); `tests/engine/test_pty_control{,_skeleton}.py` dataclass-shape assertions updated to include the new `run_dir_path` field. (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: fix/adr-035-impl-audit-p1, session: 20260514-130035-f35-impl-fix-audit-p1-p2-adr-035)

- [#876] ProcessBlock output Collection no longer pinned to input item_type. `src/scieasy/blocks/process/process_block.py:166` previously forced `Collection(results, item_type=primary.item_type)`, which broke parent-typed outputs (e.g. SRSImage→Image transformations) by failing `Collection.__init__`'s strict isinstance check with `TypeError: Collection requires homogeneous types: item[0] is Image, expected SRSImage`. The bidirectional port-type fix (#601) only patched design-time `validate_connection`, not runtime Collection construction. Now infers item_type from the actual results; falls back to `primary.item_type` only when results is empty so the empty Collection still carries a meaningful type label for downstream port checks. Adds `TestProcessBlockOutputTypeInference` (2 cases: parent-type output accepted, empty input preserves input type). (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: fix/issue-876/process-block-collection-type-inference, session: 20260514-134618)
- [#851] ADR-036 Phase 2.6 — fix audit P1 findings (saveFileTab data-loss race + new-block/note silent overwrite). `saveFileTab` in `frontend/src/store/tabSlice.ts` used to snapshot the tab BEFORE the in-flight `putProjectFile` await and rebuild the FileTab from that stale reference post-await, silently overwriting any keystrokes the user made during the network round-trip. Now the post-await branch re-reads the latest tab from the store and only clears `dirty` if the content has not diverged; if the user typed mid-flight, `contentLoadedAt` advances (the older content really did land on disk) but `dirty=true` so the next debounce saves the newer content. New `frontend/src/lib/fileExistence.ts::probeProjectFileExistence` GETs the target path before PUT for `createNewCustomBlock` / `createNewNote` in `App.tsx`; 200 → alert + abort, 404 → safe to create, other errors surface to the user. P2 #6 (createNewNote silently falls back to project root on any error) also fixed in-PR — `getProjectTree("notes")` failures now branch on `ApiError.status === 404` only. P2 #3 (rehydrated tab stuck loading), #4 (multi-tab autosave debounce cancel), #5 (lint stale-response paint) deferred to backlog issues. Tests: 2 new vitest cases in `tabState.test.ts` exercise the race with a stalled `putProjectFile` mock + interleaved `updateFileTabContent`; 4 new cases in `fileExistence.test.ts` cover the existence probe (exists / missing / non-404 ApiError / network Error). (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: fix/adr-036-impl-audit-p1, session: 20260514-131100-f36-impl-phase-2-6-fix-audit-p1-p2)
- [#840] Live-test hotfix bundle for PR #834. (a) Canvas blank on workflow modify — `workflow_watcher` now suppresses transient `kind=deleted` events when the path still exists at emit time (atomic-replace artefact). (b) MCP `get_run_status.errors` was always `[]`; engine already emits full Python tracebacks on `block_error`, the MCP layer just wasn't surfacing them — now lazy-installs a `block_error` subscriber on the runtime's `event_bus` (exposed via 3-line `_RuntimeAdapter.event_bus` addition in `api/app.py`) and returns the captured records, with a `task.exception()` + `format_exception` fallback for scheduler-level failures. (c) Logs tab "N unread but panel empty" — `unreadLogsCount` was bumped for every `block_*`/`workflow_*` event but only `block_error` produced a Logs row; the badge is now coupled to the actual `appendLog`/`consumeEvent` row append in `executionSlice`. (d) Refactor: Problems tab collapsed into Logs (`LogViewer` already shipped a level selector). Drops `ProblemsPanel`, `unreadProblemsCount`, `bumpUnreadProblems`; keeps the `blockErrors` store field for the inline BlockNode error badge. (e) `write_workflow` MCP tool now pre-validates against `WorkflowFileModel` before writing so malformed YAML (e.g. agent-written 4-field edges) never lands on disk; the GET route surfaces 422 with the pydantic error list for any pre-existing bad files instead of 500. Engine + schema intentionally untouched per project policy. (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: fix/adr-034/bugs-abc-canvas-traceback-logs, session: 20260514-005000-pr834-hotfix-bundle)
- [#810][#811] Restore mcp-bridge run() impl + MCP-spec content blocks. `cli/mcp_bridge.py::run()` now implements both attached-mode (proxy stdin↔backend socket) and standalone-mode (spawn in-process MCPServer via `runtime.make_mcp_runtime`); `mcp/server.py:233` returns spec-compliant `{"type": "text", "text": json.dumps(...)}` instead of non-spec `{"type": "json", ...}`. Both regressions were introduced by PR #808's rollback over-correction. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-810-811/mcp-bridge-and-content-block, session: 20260513-200156-fix-810-811-mcp-bridge-run-mcp-content-b)

### Added

- [#817] ADR-034 Phase 1.3 — Frontend xterm.js terminal. New `frontend/src/components/AIChat/` package: `SetupScreen` (provider + permission-mode picker reading `/api/ai/status`), `TerminalView` (xterm.js wrapper with fit/search/web-links addons), `TerminalTab` (setup→running→closed state machine), `TerminalTabs` (multi-tab strip with Ctrl+T / Ctrl+W / Ctrl+1..9 shortcuts, capture-phase listener so Ctrl+W beats Chrome's default), and `hooks/usePtyWebSocket` (locked JSON-frame protocol — `stdin` / `resize` outbound, `stdout` / `exit` / `error` inbound, no auto-reconnect). New Zustand `terminalTabsSlice` persists tab metadata across reloads; on rehydrate any `running` tab is downgraded to `closed` with synthetic `exitCode -1` since the PTY did not survive page unload. `BottomPanel` now mounts `<TerminalTabs/>` for the AI bottom tab; `App.tsx` drops the legacy chat plumbing (`chatMessages`, `aiLoading`, `aiError`, `onSendChat`, `onApplyWorkflow`). Legacy `AIChat.tsx` is left in place per Phase 1.3 scope — Phase 2 deletes it. 29 new vitest cases (`__tests__/SetupScreen.test.tsx`, `TerminalView.test.tsx`, `TerminalTabs.test.tsx`, `usePtyWebSocket.test.ts`) cover URL encoding, frame dispatch, disabled-Launch logic, "(not logged in)" hint, keyboard shortcuts, and rehydration downgrade. Backend Phase 1.2 lands in parallel; WS contract is locked identically in both. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: feat/issue-817/phase-1-3-frontend-terminal, session: 20260513-204242-adr-034-phase-1-3-frontend-xterm-js-term)
- [#813] ADR-035 draft — AI Block as PTY-tab variant of AppBlock. Rewrites AIBlock from a one-shot Messages-API call into a workflow-graph node that spawns a claude/codex agent inside an ADR-034 PTY tab. Three completion signals (MCP `finish_ai_block` + FileWatcher on declared `expected_path` + user "Mark done" button), input manifest at `.scieasy/ai-block-runs/{run_id}/manifest.json` (coordination dir, not a sandbox), outputs validated via existing IOBlock loader registry. Agent has full filesystem reach matching ADR-034 — no sandboxing per explicit user directive. Variadic ports reuse ADR-029; block UI mirrors ADR-034 Setup screen; tab survives DONE/ERROR and remains interactive. Implementation cascade (Phases 1-4) deferred to a separate ADR-035 ticket batch. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: docs/issue-813/adr-035-ai-block-draft, session: 20260513-200454-draft-adr-035-ai-block-as-pty-tab-appblo)
- [#788] Generic fallback renderer for AIChat — display_class taxonomy. Backend (`scieasy.ai.agent.stream_json.classify_for_display`) tags every `OtherEvent` with one of five stable classes (`hidden`, `meta`, `text-like`, `tool-like`, `raw`); frontend `EventRenderer` dispatches on the class instead of the legacy "Unrecognised event: <json>" fallback. New `genericRows/` folder with 4 small row components plus a reusable `<CondensedToolRow>` that #784 will also consume for native `tool_use` events. Adding a new claude stream-json kind now usually requires zero frontend changes — the structural heuristics (`text` / `content` / `tool_name+input`) handle it automatically. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: feat/issue-788/generic-fallback-renderer, session: 20260513-154519-implement-788-generic-fallback-renderer)
- [#787] Developer CLI integration — standalone `scieasy mcp-bridge` (auto-spins up an in-process MCP server when no backend is running, scoped to `$SCIEASY_PROJECT_DIR`/cwd, tear-down on stdin EOF); new `scieasy install` Typer subcommand wiring the MCP entry into Claude (`~/.claude.json` user / `<cwd>/.mcp.json` project) and Codex (`~/.codex/config.toml` `[mcp_servers.scieasy]`) plus a `--skill` install that copies `skills/scieasy/` into `~/.claude/skills/scieasy/`; new `skills/scieasy/SKILL.md` as the single source of truth for the embedded GUI agent's system prompt (`compose_system_prompt` now reads it, falling back to inline sections + warning on missing file, with the tool catalog always re-synthesised from the live registry); new `docs/cli-integration.md` linked from README. Verified live with the real `claude` CLI in a fresh project — claude called `mcp__scieasy__list_blocks` + `mcp__scieasy__get_project_info` via the standalone bridge and returned real data. ### Fixed

- [#793] Stop bottom panel from forcibly switching to the Logs tab on every engine event — `useWebSocket` no longer calls `setActiveBottomTab("logs")` when `block_*` / `workflow_*` arrive, and all `setActiveBottomTab` calls in `App.tsx` user-action callbacks (`runWorkflow`, `startFromSelected`, `handleRunBlock`, `handleRestartBlock` + their catch branches) were removed per user directive ("永远不要自动跳"). The two remaining switches are explicit user interactions: node-select goes to Config, error-badge click goes to Problems. To preserve "draw attention" UX, `uiSlice` gains `unreadLogsCount` / `unreadProblemsCount` counters that bump when events arrive while their tab is hidden; `BottomPanel` renders them as small badges next to the tab labels and clears them on activation. New tests in `useWebSocket.test.ts`, `BottomPanel.test.tsx`, `tabSlice.test.ts`. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-793-796/tab-routing, session: 20260513-161943-bundle-793-796-stop-auto-tab-switch-and)
- [#796] Restore workflow tab label and top-left title when YAML omits the `id:` field — `WorkflowModel.id` has an empty-string default in the backend schema, so a hand-edited or older workflow YAML missing `id:` round-tripped as `id: ""` and rendered a blank tab + blank top-left title (mostly hit on macOS where users edit YAML externally). `ProjectTree.handleDoubleClick` now passes the filename stem as a displayName fallback through `loadWorkflowById` to `openTab`; `tabSlice.openTab` accepts an optional displayName and prefers the workflow id, then displayName, then "Untitled"; `workflowSlice.setWorkflow` falls back to "Untitled" when id is empty. Macos live verification deferred to user; regression test `tabSlice.test.ts` reproduces the broken state-derivation path. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-793-796/tab-routing, session: 20260513-161943-bundle-793-796-stop-auto-tab-switch-and)
- [#790] MCP tool path resolution — `write_workflow`, `get_workflow`, `validate_workflow`, `update_block_config`, `get_block_config`, and `run_workflow` now resolve user-supplied path arguments against `ctx.project_dir` via the new `_resolve_project_path` helper in `src/scieasy/ai/agent/mcp/_context.py`. Previously these tools called `Path(<user_arg>)` raw, which resolved relative paths against the backend process's CWD and accepted absolute paths anywhere on disk — so workflows landed in random locations and `run_workflow` couldn't find what `write_workflow` had just written, and a malicious or buggy agent could escape the project with `../../etc/passwd`. Response envelopes now carry the absolute resolved path so the agent has unambiguous evidence of where its artifact landed. The resolution chain uses `os.path.realpath` via `Path.resolve` to handle macOS `/tmp → /private/tmp` symlinks and NFD/NFC Unicode normalisation. New `tests/ai/test_mcp_tools_disk_integration.py` adds 13 disk-state regression cases. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-790-791/mcp-paths-and-permission-mode, session: 20260513-155611-fix-790-791-mcp-path-permission-mode)
- [#791] AIChat permission_mode plumbing — the Settings panel Strict/Bypass dropdown was purely cosmetic: `useAgentWebSocket` never sent the value to the backend, and `_start_default_session` hardcoded `PermissionMode.BYPASS` regardless of the frontend setting (a Phase 5 e2e shortcut that was never reverted). STRICT mode was unreachable from the GUI; every tool call silently auto-approved. The fix adds a `?permission_mode=strict|bypass` query parameter to `WS /api/ai/chat/{chat_id}` (default STRICT), plumbs it through `_start_default_session` into `SessionMetadata.bypass_mode`, and has the frontend append the store-backed `permissionMode` to the WS URL. The Settings panel now shows a confirm dialog when changing mode mid-session (changing the store causes `useAgentWebSocket`'s effect to re-open the WS with the new mode). New `tests/api/test_strict_mode_write_workflow_e2e.py` pins the WS-to-metadata mode plumbing and the strict-mode `permission_request` emission. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-790-791/mcp-paths-and-permission-mode, session: 20260513-155611-fix-790-791-mcp-path-permission-mode)
- [#782] AIChat thinking + input UX — three related Phase 5 e2e bugs: (1) `thinking` events no longer fall through to the "Unrecognised event" branch — renderer now also catches wire frames with `raw.type === "thinking"` and shows an animated indicator (✻ Thinking…) even for empty-text / signature-only thinking frames; (2) new in-flight Thinking… indicator visible from user send until first real agent event (`assistant_text_delta` / `tool_use` / `tool_result` / `thinking` / `done` / `error`), so the chat no longer looks frozen while the agent is reasoning; (3) input textarea now bounded with `max-h-[200px] overflow-y-auto` so long messages scroll inside the textarea instead of pushing the Send button off-screen. Frontend-only fix; backend serialization already correct. Verified live in Chrome with claude-opus-4-7. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-782/aichat-thinking-and-input, session: 20260513-151107-fix-782-aichat-thinking-input-ux)
- [#775] Fix Claude subprocess launch — three coordinated bugs that prevented the agent from responding at all: stdin envelope schema (now `{type:user, message:{role,content}}` per Anthropic shape), missing `--input-format stream-json`, and bogus `@path` prefix on `--append-system-prompt` and `--mcp-config` (claude doesn't support `@file` indirection on those flags). Verified live in Chrome: agent now emits system/init → assistant → result. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-775/claude-launch, session: 20260513-001646-fix-775-claude-subprocess-launch-envelop)

- [#331] T-TRK-012: `FilterCollection` block accepts a new `expression: str` config param parsed through an AST-whitelisted evaluator (new module `src/scieasy/blocks/process/builtins/expression_evaluator.py`). Expressions run against a per-item scope of `item`, `index`, `meta`, `framework`, `user`, plus a single whitelisted `len` call — no `eval()`, no trusted-mode bypass, no DSL. Forbidden constructs (arbitrary calls, imports, lambdas, dunder attribute/name access, non-literal subscripts, `BinOp`, `NamedExpr`) raise `ValueError("Expression contains forbidden construct: ...")` at parse time so workflow validation catches the error before the block runs. Legacy `predicate_key` / `predicate_value` equality match is preserved for backward compatibility and is mutually exclusive with `expression`. Tests: 18 unit tests for the evaluator (8 positive, 10 rejection) + 12 integration tests through `FilterCollection` including empty-Collection pass-through, dunder rejection, legacy path, and mutually-exclusive mode enforcement. Spec: `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` §T-TRK-012 lines 1800-1889. - [#323] Add `SaveData` block at `src/scieasy/blocks/io/savers/save_data.py` — the canonical core IO **output** block per ADR-028 Addendum 1 §C5/§C9. `SaveData(IOBlock)` carries `direction="output"`, `type_name="save_data"`, `category="io"`, a single `data` input port whose `accepted_types` is narrowed per-instance via `get_effective_input_ports()` against the `core_type` config enum, and a `dynamic_ports` descriptor that uses `input_port_mapping` (the symmetric mirror of LoadData's `output_port_mapping`). `SaveData.save()` dispatches to one of six private module-level functions per ADR-028 Addendum 1 §C9 (`_save_array`, `_save_dataframe`, `_save_series`, `_save_text`, `_save_artifact`, `_save_composite_data`) which absorb the write logic from the T-TRK-004-deleted `csv_adapter` / `parquet_adapter` / `zarr_adapter` / `generic_adapter`. Supported extensions: Array → `.npy` / `.npz` / `.zarr` / `.parquet` (1-D); DataFrame → `.csv` / `.tsv` / `.parquet` / `.json`; Series → `.csv` / `.tsv` / `.parquet` / `.json` (single-column); Text → `.txt` / `.md` / `.html` / `.xml` / `.log` / `.yaml` / `.toml` / `.json`; Artifact → raw bytes plus a `.meta.json` sidecar; CompositeData → JSON manifest plus per-slot sidecar files in a `<stem>_slots/` subdirectory. `allow_pickle=True` opt-in enables `.pkl` / `.pickle` writes for Array / DataFrame / Series with an explicit WARNING-level security log via `logging`. `SaveData.load()` raises `NotImplementedError` (output-only). Mixed-type Collections, multi-item Collections, empty Collections, and wrong-type-for-core-type inputs all raise `ValueError` per spec §j out-of-scope rule. The new `src/scieasy/blocks/io/savers/__init__.py` re-exports `SaveData` and `src/scieasy/blocks/io/__init__.py` adds it to `__all__`. Registered as `save_data = "scieasy.blocks.io.savers.save_data:SaveData"` under `[project.entry-points."scieasy.blocks"]` so it surfaces in the block palette. Test coverage: 53 new tests in `tests/blocks/io/test_save_data.py` covering class-shape invariants, parametrized `get_effective_input_ports`, end-to-end round-trip per core type via the underlying lib (pyarrow / numpy / json / pickle / zarr — independent of T-TRK-007 LoadData merge order), allow_pickle gate (default-rejects + opt-in writes + WARNING log), mixed-type Collection rejection, and the `SaveData.load() → NotImplementedError` contract. Per `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` T-TRK-008 (Sprint A Level B PR 4 of 5, parallel with T-TRK-007). (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: feat/issue-323/T-TRK-008-save-data-class, session: 20260407-185152-t-trk-008-savedata-class-6-private-save)
- [#323] Extend `BlockRegistry._validate_dynamic_ports` (`src/scieasy/blocks/registry.py`) to accept either `output_port_mapping` (LoadData / input-direction blocks) **or** `input_port_mapping` (SaveData / output-direction blocks). Exactly one of the two keys must be present per ADR-028 Addendum 1 §C5; declaring both raises `ValueError`. T-TRK-006 (PR #321) only declared the `output_port_mapping` branch because LoadData was the first dynamic-ports consumer; SaveData is the symmetric output-direction counterpart and must use `input_port_mapping` per spec line 1497 and the T-TRK-008 prompt's locked autonomy limit. Error-message paths now interpolate the actual mapping key so diagnostics still pinpoint the offending field. The 22 existing dynamic-ports tests in `tests/blocks/test_dynamic_ports.py` continue to pass without modification. Per `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` T-TRK-008. - [#322] Add `LoadData` class (`src/scieasy/blocks/io/loaders/load_data.py`) plus six private module-level dispatch functions (`_load_array`, `_load_dataframe`, `_load_series`, `_load_text`, `_load_artifact`, `_load_composite_data`). `LoadData` is the canonical core IO loader: a single dynamic-port block whose `data` `OutputPort` accepted-types are computed per-instance from the `core_type` enum config field via `get_effective_output_ports()`. - [#320] Add `Block.get_effective_input_ports()` and `Block.get_effective_output_ports()` instance methods on the `Block` ABC plus a new `dynamic_ports: ClassVar[dict[str, Any] | None]` declarative descriptor (default `None`). The two effective-ports methods default to a defensive copy of the class-level `input_ports` / `output_ports` ClassVars; dynamic blocks (e.g. the upcoming `LoadData` / `SaveData` from T-TRK-007 / T-TRK-008) override them to return per-instance ports computed from `self.config`. - [#323] `IOBlock.run()` output direction now wraps the path receipt in a single-item `Collection` of `Text` (`Collection(items=[Text(content=str(path))], item_type=Text)`) instead of returning a literal `dict[str, str]` under a `dict[str, Collection]` signature, removing the pre-existing `# type: ignore[dict-item]` suppression on `src/scieasy/blocks/io/io_block.py`. This resolves the bookkeeping debt noted in `project_phase11_ttrk007_008_bookkeeping.md` Item 1 and restores strict typing across the IO surface. Verified zero production consumers of the old shape via grep: no `src/scieasy` code reads `result["path"]` from `IOBlock.run()` (the key has always been a write receipt for downstream observers, not a load-bearing data path). ### Removed

- [#318] Delete the bundled `src/scieasy/blocks/io/adapters/` directory (10 files: `__init__.py`, `base.py`, plus 8 `*_adapter.py` modules), `src/scieasy/blocks/io/adapter_registry.py`, and the `[project.entry-points."scieasy.adapters"]` table in `pyproject.toml`. Per ADR-028 §D1/§D2/§D4 and Phase 11 master plan §2.5 sub-1b PR-A (bundled with PR-A-2 because rewriting `io_block.py` is unimplementable while `adapter_registry.py` still imports from `adapters/*`). The legacy adapter dispatch layer is replaced by plugin-owned `IOBlock` subclasses; the TIFF and mzXML adapter logic moves to `scieasy-blocks-imaging` and `scieasy-blocks-lcms` via T-IMG-002 and T-LCMS-002 respectively, sourced from this PR's git history. Concrete core loaders (`LoadData`/`SaveData`) arrive in T-TRK-007/T-TRK-008. Also delete the now-obsolete `tests/blocks/test_io_block.py`, `tests/blocks/test_adapters.py`, and `tests/blocks/test_adapter_registry.py` test files. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: refactor/issue-318/T-TRK-004-delete-adapters-rewrite-ioblock, session: 20260407-174142-t-trk-004-delete-adapters-directory-and)
- [#310] Delete `src/scieasy/blocks/process/contrib/` stub directory and its four 1-line placeholder files (`__init__.py`, `cellpose_segment.py`, `spectral_pca.py`, `baseline_correction.py`). Per Phase 11 master plan §2.5 sub-1a and `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` T-TRK-001 (Sprint A Track 1 sub-1a parallel batch). The contrib pattern is being abandoned in favour of the plugin package pattern; the real Cellpose implementation lives in T-IMG-019 (Sprint C, `scieasy-blocks-imaging`). All four files were docstring-only stubs with zero business logic and zero test imports. `git grep "scieasy.blocks.process.contrib"` returns 0 hits in non-doc files; remaining hits inside `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` are the standards-doc description of this very ticket and are out of scope for this PR. `pytest -x --no-cov tests/blocks/` green: 342 passed, 11 skipped. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: refactor/issue-310/T-TRK-001-delete-process-contrib, session: 20260407-165842-t-trk-001-delete-process-contrib-stub-di)

### Changed

- [#318] Rewrite `src/scieasy/blocks/io/io_block.py` as an abstract base class with `load()` / `save()` abstract methods and a default `run()` dispatch keyed on `direction`, per ADR-028 §D1 and `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` T-TRK-004 (lines 914-976). Plugin IO blocks subclass `IOBlock` directly and register via the existing `scieasy.blocks` entry-point group. `name` and `description` ClassVars are preserved so the existing `BlockRegistry._scan_builtins` continues to surface the canonical `"IO Block"` / `"io_block"` identity that integration tests, workflow YAMLs, and the API connection-validator depend on. `IOBlock()` direct instantiation now raises `TypeError` per the abstractmethod contract — `tests/blocks/io/test_io_block_abc.py` asserts this. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: refactor/issue-318/T-TRK-004-delete-adapters-rewrite-ioblock, session: 20260407-174142-t-trk-004-delete-adapters-directory-and)
- [#318] Refactor `src/scieasy/api/runtime.py` and `src/scieasy/ai/generation/templates.py` to drop their imports of the deleted adapter layer. `runtime.py::upload_file` now builds `StorageReference` directly from the destination path; `runtime.py::preview_data` now reads TIFF previews via `import tifffile; tifffile.imread(path)` directly, mirroring the behaviour of the deleted `TIFFAdapter`. The `ai/generation/templates.py` IOBlock prompt no longer references the removed `scieasy.blocks.io.adapters` namespace. Both refactors are required by `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` T-TRK-004 §h step 5 ("every importer must be deleted or refactored"). (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: refactor/issue-318/T-TRK-004-delete-adapters-rewrite-ioblock, session: 20260407-174142-t-trk-004-delete-adapters-directory-and)

- [#301] Phase 11 LC-MS plugin block specification (`docs/specs/phase11-lcms-block-spec.md`, 3753 lines). Documentation-only spec authored per master plan §2.4 LC-MS PLUGIN lock. Defines the `scieasy-blocks-lcms` plugin package: 4 plain-DataFrame/Artifact types (`MSRawFile(Artifact)`, `PeakTable(DataFrame)`, `MIDTable(DataFrame)`, `SampleMetadata(DataFrame)` — **NO `MSSpectrum(Series)` or `MSRun(Array)`** per user), 19 blocks across 21 T-LCMS tickets: IO (5) `LoadMSRawFiles` / `LoadPeakTable` / `LoadMIDTable` / `LoadSampleMetadata` / `SaveTable`; external tools (2) `ElMAVENBlock` (AppBlock wrapping the user's ElMAVEN interactive desktop workflow per §8 Q-2 — no UI scripting, 30-min watch_timeout, FileWatcher picks up user exports) and `AccuCorR` (CodeBlock `language="r"` wrapping the AccuCor R package v0.3.1 via a bundled `accucor_default.R` driver script resolved via `importlib.resources` per §8 Q-1); isotope tracing USP cluster (5) `Calculate13CEnrichment` / `FractionalLabeling` / `CompareGroupMID` / `FluxEstimate` (simple `labeling_rate × pool_size` — explicitly NOT 13C-MFA per §8 Q-9) / `PoolSizeNormalize`; metabolomics analysis (6) `MetaboliteMatrix` / `MatrixPreprocess` / `UnivariateStats` / `MultivariateAnalysis` / `PathwayEnrichment` (Python-native KEGG REST default per §8 Q-6, MetaboAnalystR R wrapper deferred) / `ConsumptionSecretionAnalysis` (NEW per user, spent-vs-fresh media flux with optional cell count normalization per §8 Q-7); external plotting (1) `GraphPadBlock` (AppBlock wrapping GraphPad Prism, no default path per §8 Q-8, Windows-primary with non-Windows warning). Spec explicitly forbids adding scan-level data types, `EnumerateIsotopologues` / `MatchIsotopologues` / `ComputeMID` / `AtomPercentExcess` / `TimeCourseFit` / `TracerFateMap` (AccuCor does all of this externally), QC blocks, `ManualReview` blocks, MZmine / XCMS (user: "先实现 ElMAVEN"), and full 13C-MFA. MID long-format locked per §8 Q-3 (matches AccuCor output and the user's verbatim cytosine example). Sample-column detection heuristic per §8 Q-4 (`_KNOWN_IDENTITY_COLUMNS` ∪ `_KNOWN_ATOM_COLUMNS` exclusion with regex override). Multi-tracer support (`C13 + H2`) per §8 Q-5. Per §8 Q-11, no LC-MS block uses `dynamic_ports` — all four plugin types render via the existing `resolveTypeColor` walk with no frontend changes. 12 resolved open questions (§8 Q-1 through Q-12) capture every decision the spec agent owned beyond the master plan lock. 21 T-LCMS tickets each with the 12-subsection pattern matching `phase10-implementation-standards.md`: T-LCMS-001 scaffold, T-LCMS-002 types, T-LCMS-003..006 IO, T-LCMS-007 ElMAVEN+AccuCor, T-LCMS-008..012 isotope tracing (most-detailed cluster as the plugin USP — T-LCMS-008 `Calculate13CEnrichment` includes the Antoniewicz 2018 formula `E[c,s] = sum(n * M+n[c,s]) / n_max[c]` with the user's verbatim cytosine worked example), T-LCMS-013..018 metabolomics analysis, T-LCMS-019 GraphPad, T-LCMS-020 entry-point registration + smoke test, T-LCMS-021 isotope tracing integration test with synthetic fixtures (per master plan §8, LC-MS does NOT use the 4 imaging test images at Example/images/ — those are imaging/SRS only). Section §11 contains the full end-to-end integration test body chaining `LoadPeakTable` → `LoadMIDTable` → `LoadSampleMetadata` → `Calculate13CEnrichment` → `CompareGroupMID` → `MetaboliteMatrix` → `MatrixPreprocess` → `UnivariateStats` → `SaveTable` with no external-tool dependencies and no network calls. Package layout: `packages/scieasy-blocks-lcms/` with `pyproject.toml` declaring `scieasy.blocks` + `scieasy.types` entry-points, `scripts/accucor_default.R` as package data via `[tool.setuptools.package-data]`, and `requires_elmaven` / `requires_r` / `requires_graphpad` pytest markers for external-tool integration tests. Estimated total implementation size ~9,680 LOC across 21 stacked PRs. No ADR changes, no source/test changes — docs-only. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: docs/issue-301/phase11-lcms-spec, session: 20260407-011856-phase-11-lc-ms-plugin-block-specificatio)
- [#298] Phase 11 imaging plugin specification (`docs/specs/phase11-imaging-block-spec.md`, ~6200 lines). Documentation-only spec that codifies the contract for the `scieasy-blocks-imaging` plugin package and its 38 implementation tickets (T-IMG-001 through T-IMG-038), mirroring the structure of `docs/specs/phase10-implementation-standards.md`. Defines the four imaging types (`Image(Array)` 2D-to-6D with the t/z/c/lambda/y/x alphabet, `Mask(Image)` strict bool-dtype, `Label(CompositeData)` with raster+polygon slots, `Transform(Array)` for affine matrices), the unified `LoadImage`/`SaveImage` IO blocks (TIFF/PNG/JPG/NPY/Zarr first-class plus optional CZI/ND2/LIF extras, lazy loading at 128 MiB threshold, `SCIEASY:`-prefixed JSON-in-ImageDescription metadata protocol moved verbatim from OptEasy `tiff_adapter.py`), the flagship `CellposeSegment` block using `ProcessBlock.setup`/`teardown` to load the cellpose model ONCE per run (Q-IMG-2 CPU default, GPU auto-fallback, `torch.cuda.empty_cache()` in teardown), 12 preprocessing blocks (`Denoise`/`BackgroundSubtract`/`Normalize`/`FlatFieldCorrect`/`Rotate`/`Flip`/`Crop`/`Pad`/`Resize`/`ConvertDType`/`AxisSplit`/`AxisMerge` plus `Deconvolve` Phase 12 placeholder), 5 morphology blocks (`MorphologyOp`/`EdgeDetect`/`RidgeFilter`/`Sharpen`/`FFTFilter`), 8 segmentation blocks (`Threshold` with 8 methods, `Watershed`, `BlobDetect`, `ConnectedComponents`, the 5-block cleanup bundle), `TrackObjects` Phase 12 placeholder, 3 measurement blocks (`RegionProps` with multi-select properties param, `PairwiseDistance` for tumour-microenvironment analyses, `Colocalization`), 3 registration blocks (`ComputeRegistration`/`ApplyTransform`/`RegisterSeries`), `AxisProjection`+`SelectSlice`, 4 scalar math blocks plus `ImageCalculator` (with AST-whitelisted expression mode for FRET ratios; variadic deferred to ADR-029 per Q-IMG-5), 5 visualization blocks producing `Artifact` outputs, and 4 interactive AppBlocks (`FijiBlock` with the user's locked Windows Fiji path, `NapariBlock`, `CellProfilerBlock`, `QuPathBlock`). Twelve resolved open questions cover the TIFF metadata protocol location (Q-IMG-1), Cellpose CPU fallback (Q-IMG-2), metadata propagation under shape-changing transforms with `Resize` updating `pixel_size` (Q-IMG-3), `AxisSplit` filename derivation rule (Q-IMG-4), `ImageCalculator` 0.1.0 fixed-port subset (Q-IMG-5), `Mask` strict dtype enforcement via `_validate_extra` (Q-IMG-6), `Label` requires-at-least-one-slot rule (Q-IMG-7), `LoadImage` unsupported-extension behaviour with no fallback (Q-IMG-8), the `iterate_over_axes`-vs-direct-indexing rule (Q-IMG-9), the 128 MiB lazy threshold (Q-IMG-10), `SaveImage` length-1-vs-N path semantics (Q-IMG-11), and `RegionProps` Collection-input concatenation pattern (Q-IMG-12). Each ticket section follows the Phase 10 12-subsection contract: source ADR sections, files to create, files to modify, new tests (each ticket lists 5-15 specific test names), implementation details with code sketches, acceptance criteria checklist, out-of-scope notes, dependencies, diff size estimate, suggested workflow gate ticket title. Cross-reference table maps every ticket to ADR-027 / ADR-028 / Addendum 1 sections; dependency graph identifies the critical path (T-IMG-001 → T-IMG-002 → T-IMG-019); recommended chained PR order shows where parallel work is permitted. Universal rules section mirrors Phase 10 standards §4 with two added imaging-specific rules: optional dependencies declared in extras with `requires_<extra>` pytest markers, and metadata propagation per ADR-027 D5 mandatory. Universal acceptance criteria add a worker subprocess round-trip smoke test for every block. E2E test sketch in §11 covers the imaging-only sub-workflow against the four `K562_*_2845`/`K562_*_spectra` test images at `C:\Users\jiazh\Desktop\workspace\Example\images\` (with parens and spaces in filenames preserved verbatim per master plan §8) and acknowledges the cross-plugin extension where `ExtractSpectrum` (specified in `docs/specs/phase11-srs-block-spec.md`) consumes the masks plus the spectra branch. Block list, type definitions, package layout, entry-point registration, and all locked decisions per Phase 11 master plan §2.4 are documented verbatim — this spec makes ZERO architectural decisions, only records them. Enables the Phase 11 implementation cascade for the `scieasy-blocks-imaging` 0.1.0 release. - [#299] Phase 11 SRS plugin block specification — `docs/specs/phase11-srs-block-spec.md` (~1900 lines). Documentation-only spec defining the implementation contract for `scieasy-blocks-srs` per master plan §2.4 SRS PLUGIN. Locks one type (`SRSImage` subclassing imaging's `Image` with `required_axes = frozenset({"y","x","lambda"})` and a `Meta` model carrying `wavenumbers_cm1`, `laser_power`, `integration_time`, four digitizer parameters, and pump/Stokes wavelengths) and 11 blocks across three categories: 4 preprocessing (`SRSCalibrate` digitizer inversion + `Image→SRSImage` type conversion, `SRSBaseline` polynomial/rubber_band/rolling_ball_spectral, `SRSDenoise` PCA/SVD/wavelet/BM4D, `SRSNormalize` SNV/MSC/vector/area/peak_area), 5 component analysis (`SRSVCA` Vertex Component Analysis, `SRSUnmix` NNLS with auto-VCA fallback, `SRSPCA`, `SRSICA` FastICA, `SRSKMeansCluster`), 2 spectral extraction (`ExtractSpectrum` long-format DataFrame from Mask/Label ROIs, `BandRatio` two-band intensity ratio → 2D `Image`). No `RamanSpectrum` / `Spectrum` class — spectra are returned as plain `DataFrame`. No separate `LoadSRS` block — SRS ingress reuses imaging plugin's `LoadImage` then chains `SRSCalibrate`. Explicitly removed per user feedback: `SRSDespike` (no cosmic rays in SRS), `SRSWavenumberCalibrate` (systems pre-calibrated), `SRSMCR_ALS`, `SRSNMF`, `PeakFind`, `PeakFit`, all SRS-specific measurement blocks (`LipidDropletQuantify`, `ProteinLipidRatio`, `WaterContentMap`, `CellDryMassMap`), and any ALS-flavoured baseline correction. The spec walks the full Phase 10-style 12-subsection per-ticket pattern across 15 T-SRS tickets (T-SRS-000 package skeleton, T-SRS-001 type, T-SRS-002 through T-SRS-012 blocks, T-SRS-013 entry-point wiring, T-SRS-014 cross-plugin E2E test). Six open questions resolved: re-calibration detection via type+meta guards, lambda/c coexistence via `np.moveaxis` broadcast, `ExtractSpectrum` long format with `(region_id, wavenumber_cm1, intensity)` columns, `SRSUnmix` auto-VCA fallback when references absent, `SRSKMeansCluster` spectral feature shape, `SRSBaseline` default `polynomial` order=3. Cross-plugin dependency on `scieasy-blocks-imaging` declared one-way (srs imports imaging types; reverse forbidden). E2E integration test (T-SRS-014) consumes the four real test images at `Example/images/{K562_L_2845,K562_UL_2845,K562_L_spectra,K562_UL_spectra} (uV).tif` and exercises the full pipeline `LoadImage → Denoise → CellposeSegment → SRSCalibrate → ExtractSpectrum → SaveData`, gated behind `pytest.mark.requires_imaging`. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: docs/issue-299/phase11-srs-spec, session: 20260407-011711-phase-11-srs-plugin-spec-docs-specs-phas)
- [#297] ADR-029 preliminary: variadic port count and per-instance port editor (scope pending discussion). Reserves the ADR-029 namespace and documents the problem space for the count dimension of dynamic-port behaviour that ADR-028 Addendum 1 explicitly deferred. **Contains no architectural decisions** — every section that would normally hold a "Decision" reads "Pending discussion". The body documents the current state of `AIBlock` (30-line stub whose `run()` raises `NotImplementedError`, no port lists declared) and `CodeBlock` (163 lines, single static `data` input port and `result` output port both typed `DataObject`), explains why variadic ports are needed (concrete use cases: AI block taking N images and producing M tables, R-script ensemble averaging with variable fan-in, Python preprocessing fork with multiple typed outputs, future ensemble blocks), distinguishes the count dimension from Addendum 1's type dimension (fixed-count enum-driven types vs. variable-count user-declared types per port), and explains why the design discussion is being deferred until after the Phase 11 plugin cascade lands. Lists ten open questions Q1–Q10 each with 2–4 candidate answer directions A/B/C/D none of which are endorsed: Q1 where the variadic port list is stored (inline in `self.config`, new `self.port_config`, sidecar JSON, per-instance `BlockSpec`), Q2 how the GUI renders add/remove port controls (generic `variadic_port_list` widget, per-block React component, side panel, text-declared in script body), Q3 how validation handles variadic ports (treat user-declared like class-declared, fall back to `Any`, defer to runtime, hybrid structural-plus-runtime), Q4 how the scheduler routes through variadic ports (no change, per-dispatch effective-port read, special variadic dispatch path), Q5 how `_reconstruct_one` (worker subprocess) handles variadic ports given ADR-027 Addendum 1's typed reconstruction contract (per-port `type_chain` in payload, sidecar pre-resolved mapping, restrict to scan-time-resolvable types), Q6 whether AIBlock needs a `port_template` for the palette preview (zero ports, declared template, sentinel "+" badge, tooltip-only), Q7 whether CodeBlock auto-infers ports from script AST or user declares explicitly (manual editor only, Python AST auto-infer only, hybrid by language, side-load `block.yaml`), Q8 how `BlockSpec` represents a variadic block at scan time (single bool flag, separate input/output bools, capability enum, absence of port lists), Q9 whether variadic mode mixes with Addendum 1's enum `dynamic_ports` mapping (compose freely, mutually exclusive, compose with restrictions, defer), Q10 wire format for variadic ports in engine→worker payload (sidecar field, self-describing per-port metadata, CompositeData envelope). Scope statement enumerates what would be in scope (extensions to `get_effective_*_ports()`, frontend port editor widget, backend per-instance port storage, `BlockSpec` capability flag, validator updates, worker round-trip updates) once promoted plus what is explicitly out of scope (per-port auth, lazy port instantiation, runtime type inference, migration tooling, AI port suggestion). Adds `TODO(ADR-029)` paragraphs to `AIBlock` and `CodeBlock` class docstrings as forward pointers. Decision / Alternatives considered / Consequences sections all read "Pending discussion". Status `draft — scope pending discussion`. Hard freeze: any implementation PR that touches variadic AIBlock, variadic CodeBlock, or "add port" / "remove port" GUI controls must reference ADR-029 explicitly until it is promoted to `proposed`. ~739 lines appended to `docs/adr/ADR.md`. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: docs/issue-297/adr-029-preliminary, session: 20260407-011117-adr-029-preliminary-variadic-port-count)
- [#295] ADR-028 Addendum 1: Dynamic port override mechanism and GUI consequences. Documentation-only Addendum that introduces a minimal dynamic-port mechanism on the `Block` ABC (two override methods `get_effective_input_ports()` / `get_effective_output_ports()` + an enum-only declarative `dynamic_ports: ClassVar[dict | None]` mapping), locks the `BlockNode.tsx` GUI hardcoding removal (three `blockType === "io_block"` checks generalised to `category === "io"` plus Browse button generalisation), and **supersedes ADR-028 §D3** ("Seven core loader/saver pairs"): the six concrete loader/saver classes become two dynamic blocks `LoadData` and `SaveData` with twelve private module-level dispatch functions (`_load_array`, `_load_dataframe`, `_load_series`, `_load_text`, `_load_artifact`, `_load_composite_data`, and the symmetric `_save_*` set) in `load_data.py` / `save_data.py`. The user explicitly chose private functions over helper classes (Q-B) and enum-only mapping over a mini-DSL (Q-A). AI variadic port count and CodeBlock variadic port count are explicitly out of scope and deferred to ADR-029 (preliminary). Nine discussion-point decisions D1'–D9' (with prime marks to distinguish from ADR-028's D1–D14), four rejected alternatives (no dynamic mechanism, hidden classes with meta-palette, Pydantic discriminated union, combined variadic in same addendum). Detailed impact scope enumerates 7 backend files to modify, 4 backend files to create, 2 frontend files to modify, 5 test files to create, and an explicit "not affected" list covering Phase 10 core types / engine / other block bases / ADR-027 Addendum 1 worker reconstruction contract. Framework read-path migration: `Block.validate()`, `ProcessBlock.run()`, `workflow/validator.py`, `api/routes/blocks.py` all switch from `type(block).input_ports` to `block.get_effective_*_ports()`. Plugin IO blocks (`LoadImage`, `LoadMSRawFile`, etc.) remain static and get port colours via the existing `resolveTypeColor()` type-hierarchy walk — no per-plugin frontend work. 591 lines appended to docs/adr/ADR.md. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: docs/issue-295/adr-028-addendum-1-dynamic-ports, session: 20260407-005014-adr-028-addendum-1-dynamic-ports-overrid)
- [#293] ADR-028: IOBlock architectural refactor — plugin-owned IO pattern. Documentation-only ADR that records the Phase 11 decision to delete the central adapter registry and refactor `IOBlock` into an abstract base class whose concrete subclasses are per-type loaders/savers. The eight bundled adapters are redistributed: `csv`/`parquet`/`zarr`/`generic` merge into core `LoadDataFrame`/`LoadArray`/`LoadArtifact` implementations; `tiff`/`mzxml`/`h5ad`/`fcs` move verbatim to their target plugin packages (`scieasy-blocks-imaging`, `scieasy-blocks-lcms`, future `scieasy-blocks-singlecell`, future `scieasy-blocks-flow`). Core ships seven concrete loader/saver pairs (Array/DataFrame/Series/Text/Artifact/CompositeData; bare DataObject has no loader). The `scieasy.adapters` entry-point group is deleted (ADR-025 §6 superseded); plugins register IO blocks via the existing `scieasy.blocks` entry-point group. Pickle support is first-class but opt-in via `allow_pickle: bool = False` on LoadDataFrame/LoadSeries/LoadArray with an explicit security warning. Additional first-class format paths added: `.tsv`, `.pkl`, `.pickle`, `.npy`, `.npz`, `.parquet` for single-column Series. 14 discussion-point decisions D1–D14 plus four rejected alternatives (retrofit adapter with type_chain, subclass_of ClassVar, gradual deprecation, unified TypeRegistry-reader graph). Detailed impact scope enumerates 13 files to delete, 3 files to rewrite, 14 files to create, 9 documentation files to update in follow-up PRs, and explicit "not affected" list covering core types / engine / other block bases. Migration guide for workflow YAML files (`IOBlock(format=...)` → specific loader blocks). Enables Phase 11 Track 2 (scieasy-blocks-imaging), Track 3 (scieasy-blocks-srs), Track 4 (scieasy-blocks-lcms). 752 lines appended to docs/adr/ADR.md. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: docs/issue-293/adr-028-ioblock-refactor, session: 20260406-233129-adr-028-ioblock-architectural-refactor-a)
- [#251] Stage 10.1 Part 1: Palette research, skeleton, and design doc — adds category ClassVar on Block, source/package_name fields on BlockSummary (with safe defaults), optional source?/package_name? on TS type, TODO markers in _infer_category/_summary/BlockPalette.tsx, and 13 skipped test stubs for Agent B to implement in Part 2; includes docs/design/stage-10-1-palette.md (661 lines) with current state analysis, proposed changes, test plan, and migration notes (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-251/stage-10-1-skeleton, session: 20260406-015803-stage-10-1-part-1-research-skeleton-and)
- [#290] T-014: worker subprocess typed reconstruction per ADR-027 D11 + Addendum 1 §1. Replaces the T-013 stub in `scieasy.core.types.serialization` with full `_reconstruct_one` and `_serialise_one` implementations: each delegates to the resolved class's `_reconstruct_extra_kwargs` / `_serialise_extra_metadata` classmethod hooks (T-013) for base-class-specific fields, populates the framework/meta/user three-slot model (T-005), and uses `TypeRegistry.resolve(type_chain)` (T-012) to look up the most specific registered class. `worker.reconstruct_inputs` and `worker.serialise_outputs` are refactored to delegate per-item to the new helpers, returning TYPED `DataObject` instances (not `ViewProxy`) so block authors can use `item.meta`, `item.with_meta()`, and `isinstance` checks naturally inside their subprocesses. Lazy loading is preserved at the method level: reconstructed instances have `storage_ref` set but do not read payload data until `to_memory()` / `view()` / `sel()` / `iter_over()` is called. `worker.main()` warms a module-level lazy `TypeRegistry` singleton (`_get_type_registry` in `serialization.py`) on startup that scans core built-ins via `scan_builtins()` and attempts plugin entry-points via `_scan_entrypoint_types()` inside a `contextlib.suppress(Exception)` so a broken plugin never takes down core reconstruction. The `ViewProxy` import is removed from `worker.py`; `ViewProxy` remains as the return type of `Array.view()` for blocks that need explicit chunk-by-chunk reading. Construction failures inside `_reconstruct_one` are wrapped with the offending class name (`"Failed to reconstruct {cls.__name__} from payload: {original_error}"`) so operators can locate broken payloads quickly. 38 new tests in `tests/engine/test_worker_typed_reconstruction.py` covering `_reconstruct_one` class resolution (type_chain fallback, Meta validation, framework round-trip, user dict preservation), `_serialise_one` metadata sidecar shape, round-trip equivalence for all six base classes (Array / Series / DataFrame / Text / Artifact / CompositeData), `reconstruct_inputs` dispatcher cases (single typed item, Collection, scalar pass-through), `serialise_outputs` round-trip, reconstructed-instance behaviour (with_meta, isinstance, lazy payload), the TypeRegistry singleton helper, and construction-failure error wrapping. `tests/core/test_base_class_reconstruction_hooks.py` deletes the four T-013 stub-raises tests (`test_composite_reconstruct_raises_until_t014`, `test_composite_serialise_raises_until_t014`, `test_serialization_stub_reconstruct_raises`, `test_serialization_stub_serialise_raises`) and replaces them with positive composite round-trip tests plus smoke tests for the real `_reconstruct_one` / `_serialise_one` bodies on bare `DataObject`. `tests/engine/test_worker.py` and `tests/engine/test_local_runner.py` are updated where they asserted `ViewProxy` return types to assert the typed class instead (`Array` for the imaging-shaped payload, `DataObject` for the bare fallback). Capstone of Phase 10 — every previous ticket (T-001..T-013) was preparing for this moment. Stacked on PR #289. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-290/T-014-worker-typed-reconstruction, session: 20260406-201435-t-014-worker-subprocess-typed-reconstruc)
- [#288] T-013: six base-class reconstruction hook pairs per ADR-027 Addendum 1 §2. Each of DataObject, Array, Series, DataFrame, Text, Artifact, CompositeData gains a `_reconstruct_extra_kwargs(metadata: dict) -> dict` classmethod (returns the constructor kwargs to extract from the wire-format metadata sidecar) and a `_serialise_extra_metadata(obj) -> dict` classmethod (the symmetric counterpart that writes into the sidecar). DataObject returns empty dicts by default; Array extracts `axes`/`shape`/`dtype`/`chunk_shape` (tuples↔lists, dtype stringified); Series extracts `index_name`/`value_name`/`length`; DataFrame extracts `columns`/`row_count`/`schema`; Text extracts `content`/`format`/`encoding`; Artifact extracts `file_path` (Path↔str)/`mime_type`/`description`; CompositeData recursively delegates to `_reconstruct_one` / `_serialise_one` from a new `scieasy.core.types.serialization` module via lazy import inside the classmethod body to break the load-time cycle. The `serialization` module is a T-013 stub whose `_reconstruct_one` / `_serialise_one` raise NotImplementedError with a pointer to T-014; T-014 lands the full worker reconstruction logic, replacing the stub bodies while keeping the signatures locked. Composite empty-slots paths short-circuit before touching the stub, so T-013 ships without breaking plugin tests that construct an empty composite. Subclass overrides type their `obj` parameter as `DataObject` (not the narrower subclass) to respect Liskov with the base classmethod and assert-narrow inside the body. 39 new tests in `tests/core/test_base_class_reconstruction_hooks.py` covering per-class kwargs extraction, per-class metadata emission, round-trip equivalence on the five flat base classes, composite stub-raises delegation, serialization module importability, parametrized hook discovery on all seven classes, and the plugin-subclass `super()` override chaining pattern. Stacked on PR #287. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-288/T-013-base-class-reconstruction-hooks, session: 20260406-195928-t-013-base-class-reconstruction-hooks-pe)
- [#286] T-012: TypeRegistry.resolve(type_chain) and Meta-class validation per ADR-027 D11 + Addendum 1 §3. resolve() is overloaded on argument type: passing a list[str] walks the chain rightmost-to-leftmost and returns the most specific registered class (or None) — used by worker subprocess reconstruction (T-014) to look up typed DataObject classes from serialised metadata; the legacy resolve(name: str) -> TypeSpec path is preserved for backward compatibility with existing callers (load_class, tests/core/test_types.py, tests/architecture/test_registries.py). _validate_meta_class() runs at registration time inside scan_builtins and _scan_entrypoint_types and rejects any subclass whose Meta is not a pydantic.BaseModel subclass, declares PrivateAttr fields, or fails JSON round-trip through model_dump(mode='json') / model_validate, with clear error messages pointing at the offending class. Meta classes whose required fields have no defaults skip the round-trip smoke test per the ADR (plugin authors are expected to write their own regression test). Broken plugin Meta is logged-and-skipped inside _scan_entrypoint_types so one bad plugin does not take down the whole registry; broken core-builtin Meta raises loudly inside scan_builtins. A new register_class(cls) convenience helper validates + builds a TypeSpec + registers in one call. All six core base classes (Meta=None per T-005) pass validation via a canary test that guards against future refactors. 19 new tests in tests/core/test_type_registry_resolve_and_meta.py. Stacked on PR #285. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-286/T-012-type-registry-resolve, session: 20260406-194916-t-012-typeregistry-resolve-meta-validati)
- [#284] T-011: scieasy.utils.axis_iter.iterate_over_axes(source, operates_on, func) utility per ADR-027 D3. Iterates user-provided func over all axes NOT in operates_on, calls func(slice_data, coord_dict) for each combination, stacks results back into a new Array of source's concrete class. Memory: O(one input slice + one output slice). Serial by design (no threads, no subprocesses) per ADR-027 D8. Metadata propagation: framework derived (with `derived_from=source.framework.object_id`), meta shared by reference, user shallow copy, axes preserved. Raises `BroadcastError` when operates_on is not a subset of source.axes, when source.shape is None, when slice outputs have inconsistent shapes, or when func returns arrays with a different number of dimensions than len(operates_on); user-raised errors propagate unchanged. Imports `BroadcastError` from the sibling `scieasy.utils.broadcast` module (ADR-027 D3 referenced `scieasy.core.exceptions` which does not yet exist in the repo) so one `except BroadcastError:` clause covers both utilities. Sibling of `broadcast_apply` for the "single Array, iterate extra dims" pattern. Replaces the T-011 `NotImplementedError` skeleton from PR #262; removes the corresponding smoke tests from `tests/core/test_phase10_skeleton.py`; adds 16 per-feature tests in `tests/utils/test_axis_iter.py` covering the ADR-027 D3 acceptance criteria plus edge cases (empty extra axes, func reducing dim count, subclass preservation, metadata propagation, user-func error propagation). Stacked on PR #283. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-284/T-011-axis-iter, session: 20260406-193821-t-011-scieasy-utils-axis-iter-iterate-ov)
- [#282] T-010: scieasy.utils.constraints port helper factories per ADR-027 D4 companion. Adds `has_axes(*required)` (superset check), `has_exact_axes(*axes)` (set equality), `has_shape(ndim)` (exact rank), `has_min_shape(ndim)` (minimum rank), `has_dtype(*dtypes)` (string-normalised dtype match), and `is_2d()` / `is_3d()` convenience aliases. Each factory returns a `Callable[[Collection], bool]` suitable for `InputPort(constraint=...)` — pure Python predicates that read instance attributes only, with no I/O, no `to_memory()` calls, and no storage-backend coupling (consistent with Phase 10 Level 1 laziness). Every returned callable iterates the collection once, short-circuits on first failure, treats missing attributes as a graceful `False` (not `AttributeError`), treats empty iterables as vacuously true, and carries a descriptive `__name__` / `__doc__` for `validate_port_constraint` breadcrumbs. Replaces the T-010 `NotImplementedError` skeleton from PR #262; removes the corresponding smoke tests from `tests/core/test_phase10_skeleton.py`; adds 31 per-feature tests in `tests/utils/test_constraints.py` including end-to-end integration through `InputPort` + `validate_port_constraint`. Stacked on PR #281. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-282/T-010-utils-constraints, session: 20260406-192835-t-010-scieasy-utils-constraints-per-adr)
- [#280] T-009: ProcessBlock setup/teardown lifecycle hooks per ADR-027 D7. New `setup(config)` method runs once per `run()` before iterating the input Collection and returns opaque state. New `teardown(state)` method runs in a finally block even on exception so blocks can release resources (close DB handles, free GPU memory). `process_item` signature gains an optional third parameter `state` (default `None`) that is threaded from `setup` through every per-item call to `teardown`. The default `run()` calls setup once, iterates with `state`, and calls teardown via try/finally. Backward-compat: pre-T-009 `process_item(self, item, config)` overrides continue to work because `run()` uses `inspect.signature` (`_process_item_takes_state`) to detect the override's arity and calls with 2 or 3 args accordingly. Built-in `TransformBlock` (the only built-in that overrides `process_item`) is updated to the new 3-arg form; other built-ins override `run()` directly and are unaffected. Cellpose-style heavy blocks can now load their model once per run instead of per item. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-280/T-009-process-block-lifecycle, session: 20260406-191910-t-009-processblock-setup-teardown-hooks)
- [#269] T-004: FrameworkMeta + scieasy.core.meta module per ADR-027 D5. FrameworkMeta is a frozen Pydantic v2 BaseModel populated at DataObject construction with `created_at` (UTC), `object_id` (UUIDv4 hex), `source`, `lineage_id`, and `derived_from`; its `derive(**changes)` method implements the ADR-027 D5 propagation rule. ChannelInfo is a frozen Pydantic BaseModel for plugin Meta classes describing acquisition channels (`name`, `dye`, `excitation_nm`, `emission_nm`); lives in core so plugins compose it without forcing plugin->plugin imports. `with_meta_changes(meta, **changes)` is the free-function helper backing `DataObject.with_meta()`, which lands in T-005. The Phase 10 skeleton's NotImplementedError placeholders in `src/scieasy/core/meta/` are replaced with the real implementation; the corresponding T-004 smoke tests in `tests/core/test_phase10_skeleton.py` are removed and superseded by 22 unit tests in the new `tests/core/test_framework_meta.py`. Stacked on PR #262 (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-269/T-004-framework-meta, session: 20260406-174408-t-004-frameworkmeta-scieasy-core-meta-mo)
- [#267] T-003: PhysicalQuantity dataclass with Pydantic v2 integration per ADR-027 D6 + Addendum 1 §4. - [#275] T-007: Audit and three-slot integration of remaining 5 core base classes (Series, DataFrame, CompositeData, Text, Artifact) per ADR-027 D2 + D5. Each base class now has a `with_meta()` override that propagates its specific constructor arguments alongside the standard framework/meta/user/storage_ref slots, matching the pattern T-006 introduced for Array. Core tests that referenced the deleted subtypes use local T-007 shim subclasses (same pattern T-006 established for `Image`); `tests/architecture/` and `tests/blocks/` carry alias imports with TODO(T-008) markers. New `tests/core/test_other_base_classes_audit.py` (24 tests) regression-guards the constructor + with_meta pattern on each base class. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-275/T-007-other-base-classes-audit, session: 20260406-184210-t-007-other-base-classes-audit-per-adr-0)
- [#273] T-006: Array now uses instance-level axes per ADR-027 D1 — `axes` is a required keyword-only constructor argument carrying the axis labels (e.g., `["t", "z", "c", "lambda", "y", "x"]` for 6D fluorescence/spectral imaging). Class-level schema fields `required_axes` (frozenset), `allowed_axes` (frozenset | None), and `canonical_order` (tuple) let subclasses constrain the accepted axis sets without subclassing per dimensional combination. Adds `Array.sel(**kwargs)` and `Array.iter_over(axis)` per ADR-027 D4 with Level 1 laziness (one slice per iteration step, metadata preserved per ADR-027 D5). Overrides `DataObject.with_meta()` to propagate Array-specific constructor kwargs (axes/shape/dtype/chunk_shape). `TypeSignature.from_type()` now captures `required_axes` for Array subclasses with a non-empty schema so port-level compatibility checks can enforce axis requirements (ADR-027 D1). REMOVES `Image`, `MSImage`, `SRSImage`, `FluorImage` from core per ADR-027 D2 — these now live in the `scieasy-blocks-imaging` plugin. Internal call sites in `tiff_adapter.py` and `api/runtime.py` migrated to use `Array(axes=...)` directly; `TypeRegistry.scan_builtins` no longer registers the removed subtypes. Non-core test files that imported `Image` carry a T-008 shim (`from scieasy.core.types.array import Array as Image`) so collection stays green until T-008 lands the proper migration; `tests/core/` is fully migrated in this PR. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-273/T-006-array-6d-axes, session: 20260406-181626-t-006-array-6d-instance-level-axes-per-a)
- [#271] T-005: DataObject metadata is now stratified into three slots per ADR-027 D5: `framework` (FrameworkMeta, immutable framework-managed), `meta` (typed Pydantic BaseModel, None on the base class, overridden by plugin subtypes via the new `Meta` ClassVar), and `user` (free-form JSON-serialisable dict). Adds `with_meta(**changes)` instance method that returns a new instance with updated meta and a freshly-derived FrameworkMeta (`derived_from = self.framework.object_id`). Backward-compat: `DataObject.metadata` property and `DataObject(metadata=...)` constructor kwarg both still work and emit DeprecationWarning; both removed in Phase 11. Subclasses with extra `__init__` parameters (Array, CompositeData) must override `with_meta` themselves — T-006/T-007 own those overrides. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-271/T-005-dataobject-three-slot, session: 20260406-175948-t-005-dataobject-three-slot-metadata-per)
- [#265] T-002: ResourceManager.gpu_slots default changes from 0 to None, triggering best-effort auto-detect via torch.cuda.device_count() then nvidia-smi -L per ADR-027 D10. Existing GPU blocks become dispatchable on CUDA-enabled machines without explicit project-config override. ResourceRequest.max_internal_workers and effective_cpu property formally activated for ADR-027 D8 thread-policy context. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-265/T-002-resource-manager-gpu-autodetect, session: 20260406-171241-t-002-resourcemanager-gpu-auto-detect-pe)
- [#257] Update ARCHITECTURE.md, PROJECT_TREE.md, and docs/guides/block-sdk.md to reflect ADR-018 Addendum 1 and ADR-027 — documentation only. §4.1 rewritten for 7-type core + plugin-provided domain subtypes and 6D instance-level axes; §4.5 documents iterate_over_axes utility; §5.1 adds setup/teardown hooks; §5.4 states core/plugin boundary; §6.1 documents scheduler concurrency model with asyncio.create_task + _active_tasks; §6.4 documents ResourceManager GPU auto-detect and ResourceRequest.max_internal_workers; Appendix A gains plugin prerequisite note. block-sdk.md gains new sections on setup/teardown, domain metadata conventions, L2 fan-out parallelism pattern, and thread policy; all core-Image imports in examples replaced with plugin-package imports (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: docs/issue-257/phase10-arch-updates, session: 20260406-045449-phase-10-architecture-and-dev-guide-doc)

- Phase 4 — Block system implementation:
  - Port system: type matching (isinstance-based, inheritance-aware), constraint validation, connection validation (source→target compatibility)
  - Block lifecycle: validate() with port type/constraint checking, postprocess() pass-through, state machine with transition()
  - IOBlock: read/write via AdapterRegistry with direction config
  - ProcessBlock: base with algorithm ClassVar; MergeBlock (Arrow concat), SplitBlock (head/ratio/filter)
  - CodeBlock: inline and script modes with MEMORY/PROXY/CHUNKED delivery
  - PythonRunner: exec() for inline, importlib for script with mtime-based hot-reload safety
  - introspect_script(): AST-based run() signature and configure() schema extraction
  - R/Julia runners: helpful NotImplementedError stubs
  - AppBlock: full lifecycle with RUNNING→PAUSED→RUNNING→DONE state transitions
  - FileExchangeBridge: prepare (JSON manifest), launch (subprocess), watch, collect
  - FileWatcher: polling-based output detection with timeout and glob patterns
  - SubWorkflowBlock: input/output mapping with sequential executor stub (real DAG scheduler in Phase 5)
  - BlockRegistry: Tier 1 (drop-in .py scan) + Tier 2 (entry_points) discovery, instantiate(), hot_reload()
  - AdapterRegistry: extension→adapter mapping with register_defaults() and entry_point scan
  - RunnerRegistry: language→runner mapping with register_defaults()
  - Format adapters: CSV (PyArrow), Parquet (PyArrow), TIFF (tifffile), generic binary (Artifact)
  - Stub adapters: mzXML, H5AD, FCS with NotImplementedError
  - 69 new tests across 7 test files covering ports, IO, process, code, app, registry, and subworkflow blocks
- CI: test coverage enforcement at 65% minimum via pytest-cov (will increase to 85% as test suite grows)
- CI: PR gate check requiring tests/ updates when src/ changes

- Phase 3 — Core data layer implementation:
  - DataObject metadata handling, TypeSignature auto-generation from class MRO
  - TypeSignature.matches() for inheritance-aware type compatibility
  - CompositeData slot management with type validation (get, set, slot_types)
  - TypeRegistry with register, resolve, scan_builtins, load_class, is_instance
  - ZarrBackend — write/read numpy arrays via Zarr, chunk-aware slicing
  - ArrowBackend — write/read PyArrow Tables via Parquet, column selection
  - FilesystemBackend — text and binary file storage with byte-range slicing
  - CompositeStore — directory-of-slots with manifest.json
  - ViewProxy — lazy loading with shape/axes metadata, size warnings (>2 GB)
  - LineageStore — SQLite-backed lineage records with ancestor tracing
  - EnvironmentSnapshot.capture() — Python version and key package versions
  - ProvenanceGraph — in-memory ancestry, descendant, diff, and audit queries
  - broadcast_apply() — named-axis-aware broadcasting utility
  - iter_axis_slices() — axis-aware slice generator for Array types
  - content_hash() — xxhash-based content hashing for lineage
  - 102 tests covering types, composites, storage round-trips, proxy lazy loading, lineage, and broadcast
- [#9] Scaffold repository structure and implement interface skeleton (Phases 0-2)
- [#7] Add mandatory branch and PR commit rules to CLAUDE.md
- Workflow gate system (`.workflow/gate.py`) for enforced development pipeline
- SpecKit integration (`.specify/`) for feature-level design pipeline
- GitHub Actions CI: lint, typecheck, test matrix, import contracts
- GitHub Actions workflow gate check for PR compliance
- Issue templates (feature, bug, refactor, architecture)
- PR template with checklist
- CLAUDE.md governance: branch discipline, merge conflict handling, branch cleanup rules
